Bản Kiểm Kê Đầy Đủ và Giải Thích Từng File cho Baseline HRC 2026
====================================================================
GHI CHÚ BẢN DỊCH
Tài liệu này là bản tiếng Việt được tạo từ inventory tiếng Anh bằng chuyển đổi có kiểm soát.
Các đường dẫn, tên file, import, class/function, CLI flag, log key, nhãn như [CONFIRMED]/[INFERRED], và một số docstring hoặc snippet vendor được giữ nguyên khi cần để bảo toàn độ chính xác kỹ thuật và khả năng grep.
Nếu một câu là dữ liệu trích nguyên từ source/vendor, bản dịch có thể giữ tiếng Anh hoặc chỉ Việt hóa phần nhãn bao quanh.


1. TIÊU ĐỀ
Bản Kiểm Kê Đầy Đủ và Giải Thích Từng File cho Baseline HRC 2026

2. TÓM TẮT GỐC BASELINE
- Đường dẫn gốc baseline: /home/edward/hrc-runtime/baseline/GlobalHumanoidRobotChallenge_2026_Baseline
- Thời điểm quét: 2026-04-19T00:23:53+07:00
- Tổng số thư mục: 45
- Tổng số file: 153
- Phương pháp: quét đệ quy filesystem bằng Python pathlib trên baseline root đã chọn; mỗi file được đọc dạng bytes, giải mã thành text khi an toàn, phân loại theo path/extension/content, và cross-reference bằng Python import cùng tham chiếu chuỗi/đường dẫn.
- Các candidate baseline đã kiểm tra:
  - $HRC_ROOT resolve thành /home/edward/hrc-runtime [CONFIRMED]
  - /home/edward/hrc-runtime/baseline [CONFIRMED: thư mục chứa checkout baseline chính thức]
  - /home/edward/hrc-runtime/baseline/GlobalHumanoidRobotChallenge_2026_Baseline [SELECTED: chứa run.sh, Ubtech_sim/main.py, các YAML task, pyproject.toml, README, và package lerobot]
  - /home/edward/hrc-runtime/logs entry chứa chữ baseline bị loại vì là runtime log, không phải source baseline root.
- Tiêu chí phân loại file: extension, path, nội dung text, Python AST, CLI/main guard, field YAML task đã biết, tham chiếu command trong README, và tham chiếu tĩnh trực tiếp.
- File không giải mã trực tiếp dạng text: 17. Các file này vẫn được kiểm kê với kích thước byte, loại file, đường dẫn và vai trò theo ngữ cảnh. Phần lớn là Git pack/index hoặc cache bytecode Python.
- Ghi chú: Thư mục submodule `assets/` tồn tại trong checkout nhưng không có file trong cây baseline local này. Asset chính thức được kỳ vọng lấy từ Hugging Face hoặc một cây runtime asset riêng.

3. CÁCH ĐỌC TÀI LIỆU NÀY
- [CONFIRMED] nghĩa là thông tin đến từ nội dung file đã giải mã, source đã parse, metadata filesystem, hoặc tham chiếu tĩnh trực tiếp tìm thấy trong lần quét này.
- [INFERRED] nghĩa là thông tin là suy luận thận trọng từ tên file, thư mục, loại binary, mẫu cache sinh ra, hoặc tham chiếu source gần đó. Các suy luận không được xem là sự thật đã chứng minh bằng runtime.
- Mỗi block file gồm LOẠI, NHÃN, TRẠNG THÁI, MỤC ĐÍCH, NỘI DUNG BÊN TRONG, VÌ SAO QUAN TRỌNG, LIÊN KẾT VỚI PHẦN KHÁC, CHI TIẾT CHÍNH, và TÓM TẮT DỄ HIỂU.
- Nhãn sử dụng: [CONFIRMED], [INFERRED], [ENTRYPOINT], [TRAINING], [INFERENCE], [DEPLOYMENT], [CONFIG], [DATA], [ASSET], [EVALUATION], [UTILITY], [DOC], [SCRIPT], [NOTEBOOK], [TEST], [ENV], [DEPENDENCY], [MODEL], [CHECKPOINT], [UNKNOWN]

7. ENTRYPOINT VÀ CÁC LUỒNG THỰC THI QUAN TRỌNG
Các candidate entrypoint phát hiện:
- Ubtech_sim/main.py: Isaac Sim entrypoint that loads one task config, builds the scene, initializes Walker S2, wires IK/control callbacks, and runs the simulation loop.
- lerobot/common/policies/pi0/conversion_scripts/benchmark.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: none detected. Main functions: main.
- lerobot/common/policies/pi0/conversion_scripts/compare_with_jax.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: none detected. Main functions: display, main.
- lerobot/common/policies/pi0/conversion_scripts/convert_pi0_to_hf_lerobot.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: none detected. Main functions: convert_pi0_checkpoint, flatten_for_memory, flatten_for_npz, slice_gemma_state_dict, slice_initial_orbax_checkpoint, slice_paligemma_state_dict.
- lerobot/common/robot_devices/cameras/intelrealsense.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: IntelRealSenseCamera. Main functions: __del__, __init__, async_read, connect, disconnect, find_cameras.
- lerobot/common/robot_devices/cameras/opencv.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: OpenCVCamera. Main functions: __del__, __init__, _find_cameras, async_read, connect, disconnect.
- lerobot/scripts/configure_motor.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: none detected. Main functions: configure_motor, get_motor_bus_cls.
- lerobot/scripts/control_robot.py: Main LeRobot control entrypoint for calibration, teleoperation, data recording, replay, inference-with-recording, and remote control.
- lerobot/scripts/display_sys_info.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: none detected. Main functions: display_sys_info, format_dict.
- lerobot/scripts/eval.py: Evaluation entrypoint and rollout logic for policy/environment scoring.
- lerobot/scripts/find_motors_bus_port.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: none detected. Main functions: find_available_ports, find_port.
- lerobot/scripts/push_pretrained.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: PushPreTrainedConfig. Main functions: main.
- lerobot/scripts/train.py: Training entrypoint for imitation-learning policies using LeRobotDataset and policy factories.
- lerobot/scripts/visualize_dataset.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: EpisodeSampler. Main functions: __init__, __iter__, __len__, main, to_hwc_uint8_numpy, visualize_dataset.
- lerobot/scripts/visualize_dataset_html.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: none detected. Main functions: get_dataset_info, get_ep_csv_fname, get_episode_data, get_episode_language_instruction, get_episode_video_paths, hommepage.
- lerobot/scripts/visualize_image_transforms.py: Python executable script/module with CLI or main guard. Main classes: none detected. Main functions: save_all_transforms, save_each_transform, visualize_image_transforms.
- run.sh: Docker container launcher for the official baseline workspace.

Entrypoint và luồng training:
- Primary training script: lerobot/scripts/train.py [CONFIRMED].
- Flow: parse TrainPipelineConfig -> build LeRobotDataset -> create policy via policy factory -> create optimizer/scheduler -> iterate dataloader batches -> update_policy -> log metrics -> save checkpoints -> optional eval if configured.
- Main config files/classes: lerobot/configs/train.py, lerobot/configs/default.py, lerobot/configs/policies.py, lerobot/common/policies/*, lerobot/common/datasets/lerobot_dataset.py.
- README gives an ACT Task 4 training command using dataset.root, dataset.repo_id, policy.type=act, policy hyperparameters, output_dir, steps, batch_size, eval_freq, and save_checkpoint.

Luồng inference/deploy/teleop:
- Container startup: run.sh -> Docker image with Isaac Sim/LeRobot -> editable install.
- LeRobot operational entrypoint: lerobot/scripts/control_robot.py with control.type teleoperate, record, replay, or remote/inference-style record with control.policy.path.
- Robot bridge: lerobot/common/robot_devices/robots/configs.py registers robot configuration; isaac_sim_robot_interface.py connects LeRobot control to Ubtech_sim/Isaac Sim.
- Ubtech_sim direct loop: Ubtech_sim/main.py builds the Isaac scene and control callbacks directly, but direct scan found references to missing `source.coordinate_utils_v2` and `config/task1.yaml`, so this path needs runtime verification or compatibility fixes before assuming it runs as-is.

Luồng setup simulation/environment:
- Task YAMLs in Ubtech_sim/config define root_path, scene_usd, task_number, asset USD names, table/box/robot poses, scatter area, and grasp timings.
- source/config_loader.py loads YAML and applies scatter config.
- source/SceneBuilder.py creates table/parts/conveyor/box/foam/robot based on task_number and task-specific sections.
- source/RobotArticulation.py wraps Walker S2 articulation, cameras, joint defaults, IK initialization, and gripper/arm commands.
- source/DualArmIK.py solves the arm IK using Pinocchio and URDF; source/coordinate_utils.py converts between world and robot/IK frames.

Luồng evaluation:
- Primary evaluation script: lerobot/scripts/eval.py [CONFIRMED].
- Flow: parse EvalPipelineConfig -> load policy and env -> run rollout episodes -> collect rewards/success/done flags/videos -> compile episode data and summary metrics.
- Data replay/evaluation-adjacent path: lerobot/scripts/control_robot.py replay mode can restore environment_state from recorded dataset frames when available.

Luồng load asset/model:
- Assets: task YAMLs point to `../../assets/resources/` and named USD resources. The baseline checkout assets directory is empty locally; official payload is external.
- Model training/inference: policies save/load with Hugging Face-style pretrained directories; README references `challenge2026_baseline/Packing_Box/act/checkpoints/last/pretrained_model`, but those weight files are not present in this scanned baseline root.

Hub trung tâm nên kiểm tra trước:
- run.sh: environment/container launcher.
- README.md / README_zh.md: intended official workflows and task definitions.
- Ubtech_sim/source/SceneBuilder.py: task scene setup/reset/object state hub.
- Ubtech_sim/source/RobotArticulation.py: Isaac articulation and Walker S2 robot-control hub.
- Ubtech_sim/source/DualArmIK.py and coordinate_utils.py: IK/frame hub.
- lerobot/scripts/control_robot.py: teleop/record/replay/inference operational hub.
- lerobot/scripts/train.py, lerobot/scripts/eval.py: learning/evaluation hubs.
- lerobot/common/datasets/lerobot_dataset.py: dataset IO hub.
- lerobot/common/policies/factory.py plus policy subfolders: model construction hub.

Files with signs of being support/metadata rather than active runtime behavior:
- .git/* files: checkout metadata only.
- __pycache__/*.pyc files: generated bytecode caches; read corresponding .py files instead.
- Git hook *.sample files: stock sample hooks, not active unless installed into Git hook names without .sample.
- lerobot/templates/*.html: dataset visualization templates, not robot-control behavior.
- Some hardware robot interfaces (Dynamixel/Feetech/Stretch/LeKiwi/ROS2 teleop files) are part of inherited LeRobot support; they may be less relevant for Walker S2 Isaac Sim, but no dead-code claim is made without runtime tests.

Các điểm lệch nội bộ tiềm tàng phát hiện bằng scan tĩnh:
- Ubtech_sim/main.py imports `source.coordinate_utils_v2`, but only `source/coordinate_utils.py` exists in the scanned tree.
- Ubtech_sim/main.py loads `Ubtech_sim/config/task1.yaml`, but the scanned config files are Part_Sorting.yaml, Conveyor_Sorting.yaml, Foam_Inlaying.yaml, and Packing_Box.yaml.
- README layout mentions assets/datasets/challenge2026_baseline resources, but scanned root does not contain datasets or challenge2026_baseline weight files.

9. TÓM TẮT NĂNG LỰC BASELINE
[CONFIRMED] Năng lực xác nhận từ file:
- Docker-based runtime launch with NVIDIA/Isaac display/cache/Hugging Face cache handling.
- Isaac Sim scene construction for four competition task families via YAML configs and SceneBuilder.
- Walker S2 articulation setup, cameras, grippers, force/hand references, and DualArmIK-based arm control.
- Teleoperation, demonstration recording, replay, and policy-driven recording/inference through LeRobot control_robot.py.
- LeRobotDataset V2.1-style dataset reading/writing, statistics, video handling, transforms, visualization, and hub utilities.
- Imitation-learning training with ACT and Pi0 policy code paths plus reward/classifier policy modules.
- Evaluation rollouts and metrics collection through lerobot/scripts/eval.py.

[INFERRED] Tính chất của baseline:
- The baseline is broader than one task: it combines organizer scene/control code with a LeRobot learning stack.
- README examples emphasize Task 4 Packing_Box for teleop/data/training/inference, while Ubtech_sim/config/Part_Sorting.yaml supports Task 1 and is highly relevant for the current HRC project.
- The source tree is a reference implementation and launch/training scaffold, not a fully self-contained runtime because heavy assets, datasets, and pretrained weights are external.

Cần xác minh bằng runtime:
- Whether Ubtech_sim/main.py runs unchanged despite the coordinate_utils_v2/task1.yaml static mismatch.
- Whether all task configs load with local asset paths in the current machine without root_path override or symlink.
- Whether policy inference command works with official pretrained weights after weights are downloaded outside this scanned tree.

10. THỨ TỰ ĐỌC KHUYẾN NGHỊ
- README.md: Understand intended workflows, resources, commands, task definitions, and repo layout.
- run.sh: Understand Docker/runtime launch and mounted paths.
- Ubtech_sim/config/Part_Sorting.yaml: Understand Task 1 scene assets, table/box/robot placement, scatter and grasp parameters.
- Ubtech_sim/source/config_loader.py: Understand how YAML is loaded and scatter config is applied.
- Ubtech_sim/source/SceneBuilder.py: Understand how task scenes and object states are created/reset.
- Ubtech_sim/source/RobotArticulation.py: Understand Walker S2 joints, cameras, gripper, IK integration, and action command path.
- Ubtech_sim/source/DualArmIK.py: Understand official IK behavior and joint mappings.
- Ubtech_sim/source/coordinate_utils.py: Understand world/robot frame conversion and alignment diagnostics.
- Ubtech_sim/source/grasp_planner.py: Understand the organizer reference grasp state machine.
- lerobot/scripts/control_robot.py: Understand teleop/record/replay/inference orchestration.
- lerobot/common/robot_devices/robots/isaac_sim_robot_interface.py: Understand LeRobot-to-Isaac Walker S2 bridge.
- lerobot/scripts/train.py and lerobot/configs/train.py: Understand learning/training path.
- lerobot/scripts/eval.py and lerobot/configs/eval.py: Understand policy evaluation path.
